    16	package org.openrewrite.maven;
    17	
    18	import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
    19	import lombok.Value;
    20	import org.jspecify.annotations.Nullable;
    21	import org.openrewrite.ExecutionContext;
    22	import org.openrewrite.Option;
    23	import org.openrewrite.Recipe;
    24	import org.openrewrite.TreeVisitor;
    25	import org.openrewrite.marker.GitProvenance;
    26	import org.openrewrite.xml.AddToTagVisitor;
    27	import org.openrewrite.xml.ChangeTagValueVisitor;
    28	import org.openrewrite.xml.tree.Xml;
    29	
    30	import java.util.Objects;
    31	import java.util.Optional;
    32	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    33	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    34	
    35	import static org.openrewrite.internal.StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty;
    36	
    37	@Value
    38	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    39	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    40	
    41	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    42	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    43	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    44	            required = false)
    45	    @Nullable
    46	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    47	
    48	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    49	
    50	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    51	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections.";
    52	
    53	    @Override
    54	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    55	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    56	
    57	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    58	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    59	
    60	            @Override
    61	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    62	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    63	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    64	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    65	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    66	                    return document;
    67	                }
    68	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    69	
    70	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    71	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
    72	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    73	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    74	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    75	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    76	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    77	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    78	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
    79	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
    80	                                "</scm>";
    81	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
    82	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
    83	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
    84	
    85	                    }
    86	                    return document;
    87	                }
    88	
    89	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
    90	            }
    91	
    92	            @Override
    93	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    94	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
    95	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
    96	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
    97	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
    98	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
    99	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   100	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   101	                }
   102	                return tag;
   103	            }
   104	
   105	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   106	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   107	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   108	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   109	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   110	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   111	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   112	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   113	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   114	                    }
   115	                }
   116	                return tag;
   117	            }
   118	        };
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    @Value
   122	    static class GitOrigin {
   123	        private static final Pattern[] URL_PATTERNS = {
   124	                // SSH format: git@host:path(.git)?
   125	                Pattern.compile("^git@([^:]+):(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   126	
   127	                // HTTP/HTTPS with optional username and port: http(s)://[username@]host[:port]/path(.git)?
   128	                Pattern.compile("^https?://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   129	
   130	                // SSH with protocol and port: ssh://git@host[:port]/path(.git)?
   131	                Pattern.compile("^ssh://git@([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   132	
   133	                // Generic protocol://[user@]host[:port]/path(.git)? - catches any other protocols
   134	                Pattern.compile("^[a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$")
   135	        };
   136	
   137	        String host;
   138	        String path;
   139	
   140	        static @Nullable GitOrigin parseGitUrl(String gitUrl) {
   141	            if (!isNullOrEmpty(gitUrl)) {
   142	                for (Pattern pattern : URL_PATTERNS) {
   143	                    Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(gitUrl);
   144	                    if (matcher.matches()) {
   145	                        return new GitOrigin(matcher.group(1), matcher.group(2));
   146	                    }
   147	                }
   148	            }
   149	            return null;
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        String replaceHostAndPath(String originalUrl) {
   153	            if (isNullOrEmpty(originalUrl)) {
   154	                return originalUrl;
   155	            }
   156	
   157	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("scm:git:")) {
   158	                String actualUrl = originalUrl.substring("scm:git:".length());
   159	                return "scm:git:" + replaceHostAndPath(actualUrl);
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            // Handle git@ format (SSH)
   163	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("git@")) {
   164	                // First check if the URL already has the correct host and path
   165	                String expectedPrefix = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   166	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
   167	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, don't modify
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                // Otherwise, replace the host and path
   171	                Matcher gitMatcher = Pattern.compile("^git@[^:]+:(.+?)$").matcher(originalUrl);
   172	                if (gitMatcher.matches()) {
   173	                    String originalFullPath = gitMatcher.group(1);
   174	                    // Check if original path ends with .git
   175	                    boolean hasGitExtension = originalFullPath.endsWith(".git");
   176	
   177	                    // Build new URL
   178	                    String newUrl = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   179	                    if (hasGitExtension && !path.endsWith(".git")) {
   180	                        newUrl += ".git";
   181	                    }
   182	                    return newUrl;
   183	                }
   184	            }
   185	
   186	            // Handle protocol-based URLs (http, https, ssh, etc.)
   187	            Matcher protocolMatcher = Pattern.compile("^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://)(?:([^@/]+)@)?([^/]+)(/[^?#]*)?(.*)?$").matcher(originalUrl);
   188	            if (protocolMatcher.find()) {
   189	                String protocol = protocolMatcher.group(1);
   190	                String user = protocolMatcher.group(2);
   191	                String originalHost = protocolMatcher.group(3);
   192	                String originalPath = protocolMatcher.group(4);
   193	                String suffix = protocolMatcher.group(5) != null ? protocolMatcher.group(5) : "";
   194	
   195	                String userPrefix = (user != null) ? user + "@" : "";
   196	
   197	                // Determine if we need to add .git extension
   198	                boolean needsGitExtension = originalPath != null && originalPath.endsWith(".git") && !path.endsWith(".git");
   199	                String newPath = "/" + path + (needsGitExtension ? ".git" : "");
   200	
   201	                // Check if the base URL already matches (to preserve suffixes)
   202	                String newBaseUrl = protocol + userPrefix + host + newPath;
   203	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(newBaseUrl)) {
   204	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, preserve any suffix
   205	                }
   206	
   207	                return newBaseUrl + suffix;
   208	            }
   209	
   210	            // Return the original URL if no patterns matched
   211	            return originalUrl;
   212	        }
   213	    }
   214	}

Now I understand the pattern. The `getResolutionResult().getParent() == null` is used to check if a POM is the root POM. Let me now understand the issue and the fix needed.

The PR description says:
1. Since PR #5798, `UpdateScmFromGitOrigin` with `addIfMissing=true` updates ALL poms (root pom and all module poms).
2. They want an option to update only the root pom when `addIfMissing=true`.

Looking at the current code, when `addIfMissing=true` and an SCM section is missing, it adds the SCM section. The issue is that it does this for ALL poms (both root and modules). The PR wants a new option (like `updateOnlyRoot`) that, when set to `true`, would only add the SCM section to the root/parent pom.

Let me check the test file for any new tests related to this

   215	    /**
   216	     * Often recipes operating on multi-module projects will prefer to make changes to the parent pom rather than in multiple child poms.
   217	     * But if the parent isn't in the same repository as the child, the recipe would need to be applied to the child poms.
   218	     *
   219	     * @return true when the parent pom of the current pom is present in the same repository as the current pom
   220	     */
   221	    public boolean parentPomIsProjectPom() {
   222	        if (getParent() == null) {
   223	            return false;
   224	        }
   225	        ResolvedGroupArtifactVersion parentGav = getParent().getPom().getGav();
   226	        return getProjectPoms().values().stream()
   227	                .map(Pom::getGav)
   228	                .anyMatch(gav -> gav.equals(parentGav));
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    public boolean isMultiModulePom() {
   232	        return getPom().getSubprojects() == null || !getPom().getSubprojects().isEmpty();
   233	    }

    64	    private transient Xml.@Nullable Document document;
    65	
    66	    @Nullable
    67	    private transient MavenResolutionResult resolutionResult;
    68	
    69	    @Override
    70	    public String getLanguage() {
    71	        return "maven";
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    @Override
    75	    public boolean isAcceptable(SourceFile sourceFile, P p) {
    76	        return super.isAcceptable(sourceFile, p) &&
    77	                sourceFile.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class).isPresent();
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    protected MavenResolutionResult getResolutionResult() {
    81	        Iterator<Object> itr = getCursor()
    82	                .getPath(Xml.Document.class::isInstance);
    83	        if (itr.hasNext()) {
    84	            Xml.Document newDocument = (Xml.Document) itr.next();
    85	            if (document != null && document != newDocument) {
    86	                throw new IllegalStateException(
    87	                        "The same MavenVisitor instance has been used on two different XML documents. " +
    88	                                "This violates the Recipe contract that they will return a unique visitor instance every time getVisitor() is called.");
    89	            }
    90	            document = newDocument;
    91	        }
    92	        if (resolutionResult == null) {
    93	            resolutionResult = Optional.ofNullable(document)
    94	                    .map(Xml.Document::getMarkers)
    95	                    .flatMap(markers -> markers.findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class))
    96	                    .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Maven visitors should not be visiting XML documents without a Maven marker"));
    97	        }
    98	        return resolutionResult;
    99	    }

But wait, I need to understand the full flow. Currently:
1. `visitDocument` checks if `scm` child is missing. If missing and `addIfMissing=true`, it adds SCM and returns.
2. If `scm` child exists, it calls `super.visitDocument` which eventually calls `visitTag` for the `scm` tag.

The `updateOnlyRoot` option should restrict both:
- Adding SCM when missing (only add to root if `updateOnlyRoot=true`)
- Updating existing SCM (only update on root if `updateOnlyRoot=true`)

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/rewrite-maven/src/main/java/org/openrewrite/maven/UpdateScmFromGitOrigin.java   --old_str '@Override
    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {

            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
            GitOrigin gitOrigin;

            @Override
            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
                    return document;
                }
                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();

                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
                                "</scm>";
                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));

                    }
                    return document;
                }

                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
            }

            @Override
            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
                }
                return tag;

    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {

            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
            GitOrigin gitOrigin;

            @Override
            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
                if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(updateOnlyRoot) && getResolutionResult().getParent() != null) {
                    return document;
                }

                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
                    return document;
                }
                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();

                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
                                "</scm>";
                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));

                    }
                    return document;
                }

                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
            }

            @Override
            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
                }
                return tag;
            }'

    36	
    37	@Value
    38	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    39	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    40	
    41	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    42	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    43	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    44	            required = false)
    45	    @Nullable
    46	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    47	
    48	    @Option(displayName = "Update only root",
    49	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will only update or add `<scm>` section on the root POM. " +
    50	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will update all POMs in the project.",
    51	            required = false)
    52	    @Nullable
    53	    Boolean updateOnlyRoot;
    54	
    55	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    56	
    57	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    58	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections. " +
    59	               "Set `updateOnlyRoot` to `true` to only update the root POM.";
    60	
    61	    @Override
    62	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    63	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    64	
    65	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    66	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    67	
    68	            @Override
    69	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    70	                if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(updateOnlyRoot) && getResolutionResult().getParent() != null) {
    71	                    return document;
    72	                }
    73	
    74	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    75	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    76	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    77	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    78	                    return document;
    79	                }
    80	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    81	
    82	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    83	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
    84	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    85	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    86	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    87	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    88	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    89	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    90	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
    91	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
    92	                                "</scm>";
    93	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
    94	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
    95	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
    96	
    97	                    }
    98	                    return document;
    99	                }
   100	
   101	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   102	            }
   103	
   104	            @Override
   105	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   106	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
   107	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   108	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
   109	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
   110	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
   111	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   112	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   113	                }
   114	                return tag;
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   118	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   119	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   120	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   121	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   122	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   123	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   124	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   125	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   126	                    }
   127	                }
   128	                return tag;
   129	            }
   130	        };
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    @Value
   134	    static class GitOrigin {
   135	        private static final Pattern[] URL_PATTERNS = {
   136	                // SSH format: git@host:path(.git)?
   137	                Pattern.compile("^git@([^:]+):(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   138	
   139	                // HTTP/HTTPS with optional username and port: http(s)://[username@]host[:port]/path(.git)?
   140	                Pattern.compile("^https?://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   141	
   142	                // SSH with protocol and port: ssh://git@host[:port]/path(.git)?
   143	                Pattern.compile("^ssh://git@([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   144	
   145	                // Generic protocol://[user@]host[:port]/path(.git)? - catches any other protocols
   146	                Pattern.compile("^[a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$")
   147	        };
   148	
   149	        String host;
   150	        String path;
   151	
   152	        static @Nullable GitOrigin parseGitUrl(String gitUrl) {
   153	            if (!isNullOrEmpty(gitUrl)) {
   154	                for (Pattern pattern : URL_PATTERNS) {
   155	                    Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(gitUrl);
   156	                    if (matcher.matches()) {
   157	                        return new GitOrigin(matcher.group(1), matcher.group(2));
   158	                    }
   159	                }
   160	            }
   161	            return null;
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        String replaceHostAndPath(String originalUrl) {
   165	            if (isNullOrEmpty(originalUrl)) {
   166	                return originalUrl;
   167	            }
   168	
   169	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("scm:git:")) {
   170	                String actualUrl = originalUrl.substring("scm:git:".length());
   171	                return "scm:git:" + replaceHostAndPath(actualUrl);
   172	            }
   173	
   174	            // Handle git@ format (SSH)
   175	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("git@")) {
   176	                // First check if the URL already has the correct host and path
   177	                String expectedPrefix = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   178	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
   179	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, don't modify
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                // Otherwise, replace the host and path
   183	                Matcher gitMatcher = Pattern.compile("^git@[^:]+:(.+?)$").matcher(originalUrl);
   184	                if (gitMatcher.matches()) {
   185	                    String originalFullPath = gitMatcher.group(1);
   186	                    // Check if original path ends with .git
   187	                    boolean hasGitExtension = originalFullPath.endsWith(".git");
   188	
   189	                    // Build new URL
   190	                    String newUrl = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   191	                    if (hasGitExtension && !path.endsWith(".git")) {
   192	                        newUrl += ".git";
   193	                    }
   194	                    return newUrl;
   195	                }
   196	            }
   197	
   198	            // Handle protocol-based URLs (http, https, ssh, etc.)
   199	            Matcher protocolMatcher = Pattern.compile("^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://)(?:([^@/]+)@)?([^/]+)(/[^?#]*)?(.*)?$").matcher(originalUrl);
   200	            if (protocolMatcher.find()) {
   201	                String protocol = protocolMatcher.group(1);
   202	                String user = protocolMatcher.group(2);
   203	                String originalHost = protocolMatcher.group(3);
   204	                String originalPath = protocolMatcher.group(4);
   205	                String suffix = protocolMatcher.group(5) != null ? protocolMatcher.group(5) : "";
   206	
   207	                String userPrefix = (user != null) ? user + "@" : "";
   208	
   209	                // Determine if we need to add .git extension
   210	                boolean needsGitExtension = originalPath != null && originalPath.endsWith(".git") && !path.endsWith(".git");
   211	                String newPath = "/" + path + (needsGitExtension ? ".git" : "");
   212	
   213	                // Check if the base URL already matches (to preserve suffixes)
   214	                String newBaseUrl = protocol + userPrefix + host + newPath;
   215	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(newBaseUrl)) {
   216	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, preserve any suffix
   217	                }
   218	
   219	                return newBaseUrl + suffix;
   220	            }
   221	
   222	            // Return the original URL if no patterns matched
   223	            return originalUrl;
   224	        }
   225	    }
   226	}

)

val includedProjects = file("IDE.properties").let {
    if (it.exists() && (System.getProperty("idea.active") != null || System.getProperty("idea.sync.active") != null)) {
        val props = java.util.Properties()
        it.reader().use { reader ->
            props.load(reader)
        }
        allProjects.filter { it in props.keys }
    } else {
        allProjects
    }
}.toSet()

include(*(includedProjects + alwaysIncluded).toTypedArray())

if (System.getProperty("idea.active") == null &&
    System.getProperty("idea.sync.active") == null

    37	@Value
    38	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    39	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    40	
    41	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    42	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    43	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    44	            required = false)
    45	    @Nullable
    46	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    47	
    48	    @Option(displayName = "Update only root",
    49	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will only update or add `<scm>` section on the root POM. " +
    50	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will update all POMs in the project.",
    51	            required = false)
    52	    @Nullable
    53	    Boolean updateOnlyRoot;
    54	
    55	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    56	
    57	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    58	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections. " +
    59	               "Set `updateOnlyRoot` to `true` to only update the root POM.";
    60	
    61	    @Override
    62	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    63	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    64	
    65	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    66	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    67	
    68	            @Override
    69	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    70	                if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(updateOnlyRoot) && getResolutionResult().getParent() != null) {
    71	                    return document;
    72	                }
    73	
    74	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    75	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    76	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    77	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    78	                    return document;
    79	                }
    80	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    81	
    82	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    83	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
    84	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    85	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    86	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    87	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    88	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    89	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    90	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
    91	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
    92	                                "</scm>";
    93	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
    94	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
    95	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
    96	
    97	                    }
    98	                    return document;
    99	                }
   100	
   101	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   102	            }
   103	
   104	            @Override
   105	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   106	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
   107	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   108	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
   109	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
   110	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
   111	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   112	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   113	                }
   114	                return tag;
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   118	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   119	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   120	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   121	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   122	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   123	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   124	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   125	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   126	                    }
   127	                }
   128	                return tag;
   129	            }
   130	        };
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    @Value
   134	    static class GitOrigin {
   135	        private static final Pattern[] URL_PATTERNS = {
   136	                // SSH format: git@host:path(.git)?
   137	                Pattern.compile("^git@([^:]+):(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   138	
   139	                // HTTP/HTTPS with optional username and port: http(s)://[username@]host[:port]/path(.git)?
   140	                Pattern.compile("^https?://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   141	
   142	                // SSH with protocol and port: ssh://git@host[:port]/path(.git)?
   143	                Pattern.compile("^ssh://git@([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   144	
   145	                // Generic protocol://[user@]host[:port]/path(.git)? - catches any other protocols
   146	                Pattern.compile("^[a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$")
   147	        };
   148	
   149	        String host;
   150	        String path;
   151	
   152	        static @Nullable GitOrigin parseGitUrl(String gitUrl) {
   153	            if (!isNullOrEmpty(gitUrl)) {
   154	                for (Pattern pattern : URL_PATTERNS) {
   155	                    Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(gitUrl);
   156	                    if (matcher.matches()) {
   157	                        return new GitOrigin(matcher.group(1), matcher.group(2));
   158	                    }
   159	                }
   160	            }
   161	            return null;
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        String replaceHostAndPath(String originalUrl) {
   165	            if (isNullOrEmpty(originalUrl)) {
   166	                return originalUrl;
   167	            }
   168	
   169	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("scm:git:")) {
   170	                String actualUrl = originalUrl.substring("scm:git:".length());
   171	                return "scm:git:" + replaceHostAndPath(actualUrl);
   172	            }
   173	
   174	            // Handle git@ format (SSH)
   175	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("git@")) {
   176	                // First check if the URL already has the correct host and path
   177	                String expectedPrefix = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   178	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
   179	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, don't modify
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                // Otherwise, replace the host and path
   183	                Matcher gitMatcher = Pattern.compile("^git@[^:]+:(.+?)$").matcher(originalUrl);
   184	                if (gitMatcher.matches()) {
   185	                    String originalFullPath = gitMatcher.group(1);
   186	                    // Check if original path ends with .git
   187	                    boolean hasGitExtension = originalFullPath.endsWith(".git");
   188	
   189	                    // Build new URL
   190	                    String newUrl = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   191	                    if (hasGitExtension && !path.endsWith(".git")) {
   192	                        newUrl += ".git";
   193	                    }
   194	                    return newUrl;
   195	                }
   196	            }
   197	
   198	            // Handle protocol-based URLs (http, https, ssh, etc.)
   199	            Matcher protocolMatcher = Pattern.compile("^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://)(?:([^@/]+)@)?([^/]+)(/[^?#]*)?(.*)?$").matcher(originalUrl);
   200	            if (protocolMatcher.find()) {
   201	                String protocol = protocolMatcher.group(1);
   202	                String user = protocolMatcher.group(2);
   203	                String originalHost = protocolMatcher.group(3);
   204	                String originalPath = protocolMatcher.group(4);
   205	                String suffix = protocolMatcher.group(5) != null ? protocolMatcher.group(5) : "";
   206	
   207	                String userPrefix = (user != null) ? user + "@" : "";
   208	
   209	                // Determine if we need to add .git extension
   210	                boolean needsGitExtension = originalPath != null && originalPath.endsWith(".git") && !path.endsWith(".git");
   211	                String newPath = "/" + path + (needsGitExtension ? ".git" : "");
   212	
   213	                // Check if the base URL already matches (to preserve suffixes)
   214	                String newBaseUrl = protocol + userPrefix + host + newPath;
   215	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(newBaseUrl)) {
   216	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, preserve any suffix
   217	                }
   218	
   219	                return newBaseUrl + suffix;
   220	            }
   221	
   222	            // Return the original URL if no patterns matched
   223	            return originalUrl;
   224	        }
   225	    }

Let me submit my change. But before that, let me also consider one more thing: should the `updateOnlyRoot` also affect updating existing SCM tags (not just adding missing ones)? Let me trace through:

1. POM has SCM tag, `updateOnlyRoot=true`, it's a child POM:

Yes, because `MavenVisitor.isAcceptable()` ensures that only documents with `MavenResolutionResult` marker are visited. Let me also double-check: could there be a problem where `getResolutionResult()` is called before `gitOrigin` is set, and then `visitTag` uses `gitOrigin` but it's null? No, because the early return happens before any `gitOrigin` usage. And if we pass the check, we always set `gitOrigin` from the document's GitProvenance marker.

    16	package org.openrewrite.maven;
    17	
    18	import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
    19	import lombok.Value;
    20	import org.jspecify.annotations.Nullable;
    21	import org.openrewrite.ExecutionContext;
    22	import org.openrewrite.Option;
    23	import org.openrewrite.Recipe;
    24	import org.openrewrite.TreeVisitor;
    25	import org.openrewrite.marker.GitProvenance;
    26	import org.openrewrite.xml.AddToTagVisitor;
    27	import org.openrewrite.xml.ChangeTagValueVisitor;
    28	import org.openrewrite.xml.tree.Xml;
    29	
    30	import java.util.Objects;
    31	import java.util.Optional;
    32	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    33	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    34	
    35	import static org.openrewrite.internal.StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty;
    36	
    37	@Value
    38	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    39	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    40	
    41	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    42	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    43	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    44	            required = false)
    45	    @Nullable
    46	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    47	
    48	    @Option(displayName = "Update only root",
    49	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will only update or add `<scm>` section on the root POM. " +
    50	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will update all POMs in the project.",
    51	            required = false)
    52	    @Nullable
    53	    Boolean updateOnlyRoot;
    54	
    55	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    56	
    57	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    58	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections. " +
    59	               "Set `updateOnlyRoot` to `true` to only update the root POM.";
    60	
    61	    @Override
    62	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    63	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    64	
    65	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    66	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    67	
    68	            @Override
    69	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    70	                if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(updateOnlyRoot) && getResolutionResult().getParent() != null) {
    71	                    return document;
    72	                }
    73	
    74	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    75	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    76	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    77	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    78	                    return document;
    79	                }
    80	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    81	
    82	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    83	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
    84	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    85	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    86	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    87	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    88	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    89	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    90	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
    91	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
    92	                                "</scm>";
    93	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
    94	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
    95	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
    96	
    97	                    }
    98	                    return document;
    99	                }
   100	
   101	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   102	            }
   103	
   104	            @Override
   105	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   106	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
   107	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   108	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
   109	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
   110	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
   111	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   112	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   113	                }
   114	                return tag;
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   118	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   119	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   120	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   121	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   122	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   123	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   124	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   125	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   126	                    }
   127	                }
   128	                return tag;
   129	            }
   130	        };
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    @Value
   134	    static class GitOrigin {
   135	        private static final Pattern[] URL_PATTERNS = {
   136	                // SSH format: git@host:path(.git)?
   137	                Pattern.compile("^git@([^:]+):(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   138	
   139	                // HTTP/HTTPS with optional username and port: http(s)://[username@]host[:port]/path(.git)?
   140	                Pattern.compile("^https?://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   141	
   142	                // SSH with protocol and port: ssh://git@host[:port]/path(.git)?
   143	                Pattern.compile("^ssh://git@([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   144	
   145	                // Generic protocol://[user@]host[:port]/path(.git)? - catches any other protocols
   146	                Pattern.compile("^[a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$")
   147	        };
   148	
   149	        String host;
   150	        String path;
   151	
   152	        static @Nullable GitOrigin parseGitUrl(String gitUrl) {
   153	            if (!isNullOrEmpty(gitUrl)) {
   154	                for (Pattern pattern : URL_PATTERNS) {
   155	                    Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(gitUrl);
   156	                    if (matcher.matches()) {
   157	                        return new GitOrigin(matcher.group(1), matcher.group(2));
   158	                    }
   159	                }
   160	            }
   161	            return null;
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        String replaceHostAndPath(String originalUrl) {
   165	            if (isNullOrEmpty(originalUrl)) {
   166	                return originalUrl;
   167	            }
   168	
   169	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("scm:git:")) {
   170	                String actualUrl = originalUrl.substring("scm:git:".length());
   171	                return "scm:git:" + replaceHostAndPath(actualUrl);
   172	            }
   173	
   174	            // Handle git@ format (SSH)
   175	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("git@")) {
   176	                // First check if the URL already has the correct host and path
   177	                String expectedPrefix = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   178	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
   179	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, don't modify
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                // Otherwise, replace the host and path
   183	                Matcher gitMatcher = Pattern.compile("^git@[^:]+:(.+?)$").matcher(originalUrl);
   184	                if (gitMatcher.matches()) {
   185	                    String originalFullPath = gitMatcher.group(1);
   186	                    // Check if original path ends with .git
   187	                    boolean hasGitExtension = originalFullPath.endsWith(".git");
   188	
   189	                    // Build new URL
   190	                    String newUrl = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   191	                    if (hasGitExtension && !path.endsWith(".git")) {
   192	                        newUrl += ".git";
   193	                    }
   194	                    return newUrl;
   195	                }
   196	            }
   197	
   198	            // Handle protocol-based URLs (http, https, ssh, etc.)
   199	            Matcher protocolMatcher = Pattern.compile("^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://)(?:([^@/]+)@)?([^/]+)(/[^?#]*)?(.*)?$").matcher(originalUrl);
   200	            if (protocolMatcher.find()) {
   201	                String protocol = protocolMatcher.group(1);
   202	                String user = protocolMatcher.group(2);
   203	                String originalHost = protocolMatcher.group(3);
   204	                String originalPath = protocolMatcher.group(4);
   205	                String suffix = protocolMatcher.group(5) != null ? protocolMatcher.group(5) : "";
   206	
   207	                String userPrefix = (user != null) ? user + "@" : "";
   208	
   209	                // Determine if we need to add .git extension
   210	                boolean needsGitExtension = originalPath != null && originalPath.endsWith(".git") && !path.endsWith(".git");
   211	                String newPath = "/" + path + (needsGitExtension ? ".git" : "");
   212	
   213	                // Check if the base URL already matches (to preserve suffixes)
   214	                String newBaseUrl = protocol + userPrefix + host + newPath;
   215	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(newBaseUrl)) {
   216	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, preserve any suffix
   217	                }
   218	
   219	                return newBaseUrl + suffix;
   220	            }
   221	
   222	            // Return the original URL if no patterns matched
   223	            return originalUrl;
   224	        }
   225	    }
   226	}
   227
